# API 端点测试报告

生成时间: 2026-04-20 16:53:15

## 端点汇总

总计调用次数: 14
唯一端点数量: 3

***

### 1. GET /

- **描述**: 健康检查端点
- **测试用例**: 服务健康检查
- **调用次数**: 1
- **状态码**: 200
- **响应数据**:

```json
{
  "message": "Welcome to FWWB A12 API (Role D: QA & Teacher Agent)",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "docs": "/docs",
  "endpoints": [
    "/api/v1/chat/chat (POST) - Main QA/Teacher Interface",
    "/api/v1/chat/session/start (POST) - Start Learning/Preview",
    "/api/v1/chat/session/{id}/preview (GET) - Check Video Generation",
    "/api/v1/student/profile (GET/POST) - Manage Student Profile",
    "/api/v1/qa/retrieve (POST) - Retrieval API"
  ]
}
```

### 2. POST /api/v1/chat/session/start

- **描述**: 启动聊天会话
- **测试用例**: Direct RAG - 简单知识库查询
- **调用次数**: 7
- **状态码**: 200
- **响应数据**:

```json
{
  "session_id": "sess_929da771",
  "status": "active",
  "message": "Learning session started.",
  "task_id": null,
  "start_node": {
    "node_id": "node_1",
    "title": "Introduction"
  }
}
```

## 测试用例与端点对应关系

### 服务健康检查

- **GET /**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "message": "Welcome to FWWB A12 API (Role D: QA & Teacher Agent)",
    "version": "0.1.0",
    "docs": "/docs",
    "endpoints": [
      "/api/v1/chat/chat (POST) - Main QA/Teacher Interface",
      "/api/v1/chat/session/start (POST) - Start Learning/Preview",
      "/api/v1/chat/session/{id}/preview (GET) - Check Video Generation",
      "/api/v1/student/profile (GET/POST) - Manage Student Profile",
      "/api/v1/qa/retrieve (POST) - Retrieval API"
    ]
  }
  ```

### Direct RAG - 简单知识库查询

- **POST /api/v1/chat/session/start**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "session_id": "sess_929da771",
    "status": "active",
    "message": "Learning session started.",
    "task_id": null,
    "start_node": {
      "node_id": "node_1",
      "title": "Introduction"
    }
  }
  ```
- **GET /api/v1/chat/sse**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "events": [
      {
        "type": "status",
        "content": "正在分析意图...",
        "timestamp": "2026-04-20T16:45:34.732731"
      },
      {
        "type": "status",
        "content": "正在检索本地知识库...",
        "timestamp": "2026-04-20T16:45:36.568087"
      },
      {
        "type": "sources",
        "content": [
          {
            "node_id": "node_ch1_sec7",
  ```

### Direct RAG - 带来源的知识查询

- **POST /api/v1/chat/session/start**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "session_id": "sess_c32dfcf2",
    "status": "active",
    "message": "Learning session started.",
    "task_id": null,
    "start_node": {
      "node_id": "node_1",
      "title": "Introduction"
    }
  }
  ```
- **GET /api/v1/chat/sse**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:

- **POST /api/v1/chat/session/start**
- **GET /api/v1/chat/sse**
  - 状态码: 200

### Web Search - 时间敏感查询

- **POST /api/v1/chat/session/start**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "session_id": "sess_2ff331dc",
    "status": "active",
    "message": "Learning session started.",
    "task_id": null,
    "start_node": {
      "node_id": "node_1",
      "title": "Introduction"
    }
  }
  ```
- **GET /api/v1/chat/sse**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "events": [
      {
        "type": "status",
        "content": "正在分析意图...",
  ```

  ```json
  {
    "session_id": "sess_5612eb34",
  ```

  ```json
          "comment": "Great question! This helps clarify key concepts.",
          "dimensions": {
            "clarity": 4,
            "depth": 5,
            "relevance": 5
          }
        },
        "timestamp": "2026-04-20T16:52:27.737526"
      }
    ],
    "event_count": 109
  }
  ```

### 错误处理 - 空查询

- **POST /api/v1/chat/session/start**
  - 状态码: 200
  - 响应数据:
  ```json
  {
    "session_id": "sess_053cafc6",
    "status": "active",
    "message": "Learning session started.",
    "task_id": null,
    "start_node": {
      "node_id": "node_1",
      "title": "Introduction"
    }
  }
  ```
